       2562 +              document.getElementById('viewsMax').value = max > 0 ? max : '';

       2577 +              updateActiveFilters();

  def detect_ai_video(title, description, tags):
      text = f"{title} {description} {' '.join(tags)}".lower()
      for kw in ai_keywords:
          if kw in text:
              return True, kw
      return False, None

       2803 +          // ä»è§†é¢‘æ ‡é¢˜æå–è¯é¢˜å…³é”®è¯
       2804 +          function extractTopics(videos) {
       2805 +              const wordCount = {};
       2806 +              const stopWords = ['çš„', 'æ˜¯', 'åœ¨', 'äº†', 'å’Œ', 'ä¸', 'æˆ–', 'è¿™', 'é‚£', 'æœ‰', 'ä¸º',
            + 'ä»¥', 'åŠ', 'ç­‰', 'the', 'a', 'an', 'is', 'are', 'to', 'for', 'and', 'or', 'in', 'on', 'at'];
       2807 +
       2808 +              videos.forEach(v => {
       2809 +                  // ç®€å•åˆ†è¯ï¼šæŒ‰ç©ºæ ¼å’Œæ ‡ç‚¹åˆ†å‰²
       2810 +                  const words = (v.title ||
            + '').split(/[\s,ï¼Œã€‚ï¼ï¼Ÿã€ï¼š:;\-\[\]ã€ã€‘()ï¼ˆï¼‰]+/).filter(w => w.length >= 2);
       2811 +                  words.forEach(word => {
       2812 +                      const w = word.toLowerCase();
       2813 +                      if (!stopWords.includes(w) && w.length <= 10) {
       2814 +                          wordCount[w] = (wordCount[w] || 0) + 1;
       2815 +                      }
       2816 +                  });
       2817 +              });
       2818 +
       2819 +              // è¿”å›å‡ºç°æ¬¡æ•°>=3çš„å…³é”®è¯
       2820 +              return Object.entries(wordCount)
       2821 +                  .filter(([_, count]) => count >= 3)
       2822 +                  .sort((a, b) => b[1] - a[1])
       2823 +                  .slice(0, 50)
       2824 +                  .map(([word, count]) => ({ word, count }));
       2825 +          }
       2826 +
       2827 +          // æ›´æ–°æ—¶é•¿åˆ†å¸ƒå›¾è¡¨
       2828 +          function updateDurationChart(distribution, videos) {
       2829 +              const container = document.getElementById('durationChart');
       2830 +              if (!container) return;
       2831 +
       2832 +              // è®¡ç®—æ›´è¯¦ç»†çš„æ—¶é•¿åˆ†å¸ƒ
       2833 +              const durationBuckets = {
       2834 +                  '0-1åˆ†é’Ÿ': { min: 0, max: 60, count: 0, views: 0 },
       2835 +                  '1-3åˆ†é’Ÿ': { min: 60, max: 180, count: 0, views: 0 },
       2836 +                  '3-5åˆ†é’Ÿ': { min: 180, max: 300, count: 0, views: 0 },
       2837 +                  '5-10åˆ†é’Ÿ': { min: 300, max: 600, count: 0, views: 0 },
       2838 +                  '10-20åˆ†é’Ÿ': { min: 600, max: 1200, count: 0, views: 0 },
       2839 +                  '20-30åˆ†é’Ÿ': { min: 1200, max: 1800, count: 0, views: 0 },
       2840 +                  '30åˆ†é’Ÿ+': { min: 1800, max: Infinity, count: 0, views: 0 }
       2841 +              };
       2842 +
       2843 +              videos.forEach(v => {
       2844 +                  const seconds = v.durationSeconds || 0;
       2845 +                  for (const [label, bucket] of Object.entries(durationBuckets)) {
       2846 +                      if (seconds >= bucket.min && seconds < bucket.max) {
       2847 +                          bucket.count++;
       2848 +                          bucket.views += v.views || 0;
       2849 +                          break;
       2850 +                      }
       2851 +                  }
       2852 +              });
       2853 +
       2854 +              // æ‰¾å‡ºæœ€é«˜å¹³å‡æ’­æ”¾é‡çš„æ—¶é•¿åŒºé—´
       2855 +              let maxAvgViews = 0;
       2856 +              Object.values(durationBuckets).forEach(b => {
       2857 +                  b.avgViews = b.count > 0 ? Math.round(b.views / b.count) : 0;
       2858 +                  if (b.avgViews > maxAvgViews) maxAvgViews = b.avgViews;
       2859 +              });
       2860 +
       2861 +              // æ¸²æŸ“å›¾è¡¨

       2863 +                  const widthPct = maxAvgViews > 0 ? (bucket.avgViews / maxAvgViews * 100) : 0;
       2864 +                  const isTop = bucket.avgViews === maxAvgViews && bucket.count > 0;
       2865 +                  const supplyPct = videos.length > 0 ? (bucket.count / videos.length *
            + 100).toFixed(1) : 0;
       2866 +
       2867 +                  return `
       2868 +                      <div class="time-bar-row">
       2869 +                          <span class="time-label">${label}</span>
       2870 +                          <div class="time-bar-container">
       2871 +                              <div class="time-bar" style="width: ${widthPct}%; background:

       2872 +                                  ${bucket.avgViews > 10000 ? formatNumber(bucket.avgViews) :

       2874 +                          </div>
       2875 +                          <span class="time-meta">ä¾›ç»™ ${supplyPct}%</span>
       2876 +                      </div>
       2877 +                  `;
       2878 +              }).join('');
       2879 +          }

       2881 +          // æ›´æ–°æ—¶é—´è¶‹åŠ¿

       2907 +                  return;
       2908 +              }
       2909 +
       2910 +              const maxViews = Math.max(...sortedMonths.map(([_, d]) => d.views));
       2911 +

       2913 +                  const widthPct = maxViews > 0 ? (data.views / maxViews * 100) : 0;

       2915 +

       2917 +                      <div class="time-bar-row">
       2918 +                          <span class="time-label">${month}</span>

       2925 +                      </div>
       2926 +                  `;
       2927 +              }).join('');
       2928 +          }
